August 1, 2017 &#8212; Apple</font><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:pt">&#174;</sup></font><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;">&#32;today announced financial results for its fiscal 2017 third quarter ended July 1, 2017. The Company posted quarterly revenue of $45.4 billion and quarterly earnings per diluted share of $1.67. These results compare to revenue of $42.4 billion and earnings per diluted share of $1.42 in the year-ago quarter. International sales accounted for 61 percent of the quarter&#8217;s revenue.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;">&#8220;With revenue up 7 percent year-over-year, we&#8217;re happy to report our third consecutive quarter of accelerating growth and an all-time quarterly record for Services revenue,&#8221; said Tim Cook, Apple&#8217;s CEO. &#8220;We hosted an incredibly successful Worldwide Developers Conference in June, and we&#8217;re very excited about the advances in iOS, macOS, watchOS and tvOS coming this fall.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;">&#8220;We reported unit and revenue growth in all our product categories in the June quarter, driving 17 percent growth in earnings per share,&#8221; said Luca Maestri, Apple&#8217;s CFO. &#8220;We also returned $11.7 billion to investors during the quarter, bringing cumulative capital returns under our program to almost $223 billion.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;">Apple is providing the following guidance for its fiscal 2017 fourth quarter:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;
